lineofabidines1 = {
    name = Uyu_u_n
    dynasty = dynasty_abidines
    religion = faith_jelut
    culture = jelut

    trait = bossy


    6545.1.24 = {
        birth = yes
    }

    6450.1.20 = {
        add_spouse = lineofabidines1wife
    }

    6561.1.24 = {
        trait = arrogant
        trait = temperate
        trait = fickle
    }

    6584.3.16 = {
        give_nickname = nick_the_lord_of_realm
        effect = {
            add_character_flag = had_nickname_event
        }
    }

    6598.11.18 = {
        effect = {
            adopt = character:lineofabidines17

            create_character_memory = {
                type = adopted_a_child
                participants = {
                    child = character:lineofabidines17
                }
            }
        }
    }

    6623.8.27 = {
        death = {
            death_reason = death_natural_causes
        }
    }
}
